// ==UserScript== // @id iitc-plugin-ingress-guard@hunter // @name IITC plugin: Ingress Guardian // @category Layer // @version 0.2.4.20161003.4825 // @namespace https://github.com/jonatkins/ingress-intel-total-conversion // @updateURL https://ingress-guard.tk/plugins/{{ token }}achievements_plugin.meta.js // @downloadURL https://ingress-guard.tk/plugins/{{ token }}achievements_plugin.user.js // @description Show achievements on the map. // @include https://*.ingress.com/intel* // @include http://*.ingress.com/intel* // @match https://*.ingress.com/intel* // @match http://*.ingress.com/intel* // @include https://*.ingress.com/mission/* // @include http://*.ingress.com/mission/* // @match https://*.ingress.com/mission/* // @match http://*.ingress.com/mission/* // @grant none // ==/UserScript== function wrapper(plugin_info) { // ensure plugin framework is there, even if iitc is not yet loaded if (typeof window.plugin !== 'function') window.plugin = function() {}; //PLUGIN AUTHORS: writing a plugin outside of the IITC build environment? if so, delete these lines!! //(leaving them in place might break the 'About IITC' page or break update checks) plugin_info.buildName = 'iitc'; plugin_info.dateTimeVersion = '20162912.6608'; plugin_info.pluginId = 'iitc-plugin-ingress-guard'; //END PLUGIN AUTHORS NOTE // PLUGIN START //////////////////////////////////////////////////////// // use own namespace for plugin window.plugin.ingressGuard = function() {}; window.plugin.ingressGuard.NAME_WIDTH = 80; window.plugin.ingressGuard.NAME_HEIGHT = 23; window.plugin.ingressGuard.labelLayers = {}; window.plugin.ingressGuard.infoLayer = {}; window.plugin.ingressGuard.setupCSS = function() { $(''); $('head').append(''); } plugin.ingressGuard.onClickListener = function(event) { var guid = event.target.options.guid; var marker = event.target; if (marker.options.desc) { plugin.ingressGuard.playerPopup.setContent(marker.options.desc); plugin.ingressGuard.playerPopup.setLatLng(marker.getLatLng()); map.openPopup(plugin.ingressGuard.playerPopup); } window.renderPortalDetails(guid); }; window.plugin.ingressGuard.ago = function(date) { var seconds = Math.floor((new Date() - date) / 1000); var interval = Math.floor(seconds / 31536000); if (interval > 1) { return interval + " years"; } interval = Math.floor(seconds / 86400); if (interval > 1) { return interval + " days"; } interval = Math.floor(seconds / 3600); if (interval > 1) { return interval + " hours"; } interval = Math.floor(seconds / 60); if (interval > 1) { return interval + " minutes"; } return Math.floor(seconds) + " seconds"; } window.plugin.ingressGuard.DeadLine = function(timestamp) { var d = Math.floor(Math.floor((Date.now() - timestamp) / 1000) / 86400); if (d < 90) { var dl = 7776000000 + timestamp; } else if (150 > d && d >= 90) { var dl = 12960000000 + timestamp; } else { var dl = 3484318400467; } return dl } window.plugin.ingressGuard.addLabel = function(guid, features) { var isTouchDev = window.isTouchDevice(); var previousLayer = window.plugin.ingressGuard.labelLayers[guid]; var ago = plugin.ingressGuard.ago; var now = new Date().getTime(); if (!previousLayer) { var d = Math.floor(Math.floor((Date.now() - features.timestamp) / 1000) / 86400); var portalName = 'Days ' + d; var latLng = { lat: features.late6 / 1E6, lng: features.lnge6 / 1E6 } // tooltip for marker - no HTML - and not shown on touchscreen devices var tooltip = isTouchDev ? '' : (features.player + ', ' + d + ' days ago'); // popup for marker var popup = $('
') .addClass('plugin-ingress-guard-popup'); $('') .addClass('nickname ' + (features.team === 2 ? 'res' : 'enl')) .css('font-weight', 'bold') .text(features.player) .appendTo(popup); popup.append('
Player achievements') popup .append('
') .append(features.name) .append('
') .append(document.createTextNode(ago(features.timestamp, now))) .append('
') .append('DeadLine: ' + window.unixTimeToString(plugin.ingressGuard.DeadLine(features.timestamp), true)); if (features.team == 1) { if (d < 85) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconEnl70(); } else if (d >= 85 && d <= 90) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconEnl85(); } else if (d > 90 && d <= 145) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconEnl90(); } else if (d > 145 && d <= 150) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconEnl145(); } else if (d > 150) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconEnl150(); } } else if (features.team == 2) { if (d < 85) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconRes70(); } else if (d > 85 && d <= 90) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconRes85(); } else if (d > 90 && d <= 145) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconRes90(); } else if (d > 145 && d <= 150) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconRes145(); } else if (d > 150) { var icon = new plugin.ingressGuard.iconRes150(); } } var label = L.marker(latLng, { icon: icon, desc: popup[0], title: tooltip, guid: features.pguid }); label.addEventListener('spiderfiedclick', plugin.ingressGuard.onClickListener); window.plugin.ingressGuard.labelLayers[guid] = label; label.addTo(features.team === 2 ? plugin.ingressGuard.Res : plugin.ingressGuard.Enl); window.registerMarkerForOMS(label); if (!isTouchDev) { window.setupTooltips($(label._icon)); } } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.renderPlayerAchievements = function(data) { var n = 'Achievement counts: ' + data.length; counts = ''; for (var portal in data) { detail = data[portal]; d = Math.floor(Math.floor((Date.now() - detail.timestamp) / 1000) / 86400); counts += ''; } counts += '
Portal NameDaysDate
' + detail.name.substring(0, 30) + '' + d + '' + window.unixTimeToString(detail.timestamp, true) + '
' if (window.isSmartphone()) { window.show('plugin-ingressGuard'); $('
' + '
' + n + '
' + counts + '
').appendTo(document.body); } else { dialog({ html: '
' + counts + '
', title: n, width: 'auto' }); } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.getPlayerAchievements = function(player) { $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/api", data: JSON.stringify({ iitc_player: window.PLAYER.nickname, player: player, request: "player", token: "{{ token }}", }), type: 'POST', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) { var portals = response.result.achievements; plugin.ingressGuard.renderPlayerAchievements(portals); } ); } window.plugin.ingressGuard.updatePortalLabels = function() { if (map.hasLayer(plugin.ingressGuard.Att)) { var attention = true; } else { var attention = false; } var latlngCenter = window.map.getCenter(); var zoom = window.map.getZoom(); var portalPoints = {}; var user_checked = map.hasLayer(plugin.ingressGuard.UPD) ? true : false; $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/api", data: JSON.stringify({ iitc_player: window.PLAYER.nickname, request: "achievements", attention: attention, team: "all", late6: latlngCenter.lat * 1E6, lnge6: latlngCenter.lng * 1E6, zoom: zoom, days: 70, user_checked: user_checked, token: "{{ token }}", }), type: 'POST', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) { var portals = response.result.achievements; $.each(portals, function(index, feature) { guid = feature.pguid; window.plugin.ingressGuard.addLabel(guid, feature); }); } ); } window.plugin.ingressGuard.PortalDaysDetails = function() { if (window.selectedPortal && window.portals[window.selectedPortal]) { var p = window.portals[window.selectedPortal].getLatLng(); var details_cached = plugin.ingressGuard.infoLayer[window.selectedPortal]; if (details_cached) { plugin.ingressGuard.renderPortalDetails(details_cached); } else { $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/api", data: JSON.stringify({ iitc_player: window.PLAYER.nickname, request: "portal", late6: Math.round(p.lat * 1E6), lnge6: Math.round(p.lng * 1E6), token: "{{ token }}", }), type: 'POST', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) { var details = response.result.portal[0]; plugin.ingressGuard.infoLayer[window.selectedPortal] = details; plugin.ingressGuard.renderPortalDetails(details); } ); } } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.PortalDaysDetailsFromCache = function() { if (window.selectedPortal && window.portals[window.selectedPortal]) { var details_cached = plugin.ingressGuard.infoLayer[window.selectedPortal]; if (details_cached) { plugin.ingressGuard.renderPortalDetails(details_cached); } } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.renderPortalDetails = function(details) { if (details) { var ada = ''; if (details.ada) { var ada = ' Ada (Jarvis) detected'; } var ago = plugin.ingressGuard.ago; var now = new Date().getTime(); var pd = document.getElementById('portaldetails'); $('
').css('color', 'darkorange').append('Captured ' + ago(details.timestamp, now) + ' ago at ' + window.unixTimeToString(details.timestamp, true) + ' by ' + details.player + '' + ada) .append('
') .append('Address: ' + details.address) .append('
') .append('DeadLine: ' + window.unixTimeToString(plugin.ingressGuard.DeadLine(details.timestamp), true)) .append('
') .insertAfter($(pd).find('.imgpreview'));; } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.delayedUpdatePortalLabels = function(wait) { if (map.hasLayer(plugin.ingressGuard.Enl) || map.hasLayer(plugin.ingressGuard.Res)) { if (window.plugin.ingressGuard.timer === undefined) { window.plugin.ingressGuard.timer = setTimeout(function() { window.plugin.ingressGuard.timer = undefined; if (map.getZoom() > 8) { window.plugin.ingressGuard.updatePortalLabels(); } }, wait * 1000); } } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.UpdatePortalDetails = function(data) { if (data) { if (data.details.team == 'N') { $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/api", data: JSON.stringify({ iitc_player: window.PLAYER.nickname, request: "portal_check", portaldata: data.details, token: "{{ token }}", }), type: 'POST', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) {} ); } } if (map.hasLayer(plugin.ingressGuard.PD)) { window.plugin.ingressGuard.PortalDaysDetails(); } } // player search window.plugin.ingressGuard.searchPlayerRequest = function(player) { $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/api", data: JSON.stringify({ iitc_player: window.PLAYER.nickname, request: "player_info", player: player, token: "{{ token }}", }), type: 'POST', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) { var details = response.result.player_info; plugin.ingressGuard.renderPlayerSearch(details); } ); } window.plugin.ingressGuard.getAgentProfile = function(player) { $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/api", data: JSON.stringify({ iitc_player: window.PLAYER.nickname, request: "get_profile", player: player, token: "{{ token }}", }), type: 'POST', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) { var details = response.result.profile; plugin.ingressGuard.renderAgentProfile(details); } ); } window.plugin.ingressGuard.renderAgentProfile = function(data) { if (data.error) { if (window.isSmartphone()) { window.show('plugin-ingressGuard'); $('
' + '
Error

' + data.error + '

').appendTo(document.body); } else { dialog({ html: '
' + data.error + '
', title: 'Error', width: 'auto' }); } } else { counts = '

Agent ' + data.playername + ' L' + data.lvl + ' AP:' + data.ap + '

'; counts += ''; for (var badge in data.badges) { badge = data.badges[badge]; counts += ''; } counts += '
GraduateMedalAwarded
' + badge.title + '' + window.unixTimeToString(badge.timestampAwarded, true) + '
' if (window.isSmartphone()) { window.show('plugin-ingressGuard'); $('
' + '
' + data.playername + '
' + counts + '
').appendTo(document.body); } else { dialog({ html: '
' + counts + '
', title: 'Profile of agent ' + data.playername, width: 'auto' }); } } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.renderPlayerSearch = function(data) { var n = data.length; counts = ''; for (var player in data) { detail = data[player]; counts += ''; } counts += '
Agent nameLast ActivityPortal
' + detail.player + '' + window.unixTimeToString(detail.timestamp, true) + '' + detail.name.substring(0, 10) + '
' if (window.isSmartphone()) { window.show('plugin-ingressGuard'); $('
' + '
' + n + '
' + counts + '
').appendTo(document.body); } else { dialog({ html: '
' + counts + '
', title: 'Players counts: ' + n, width: 'auto' }); } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.searchPlayer = function() { var msg = $.trim($('#player_search').val()); if (!msg || msg === '') return; if (msg) { plugin.ingressGuard.searchPlayerRequest(msg); } } // Find player by name window.plugin.ingressGuard.searchDialog = function() { var html = '
' + '' + '
' + '
' + 'Search player by name' + '
'; if (window.isSmartphone()) { window.show('plugin-ingressGuard-Search'); $('
' + html + '
').appendTo(document.body); } else { dialog({ html: html, id: 'plugin-ingressGuard-options', dialogClass: 'ui-dialog-ingressGuardSet', title: 'Guardian Player Search' }); } } window.plugin.ingressGuard.onPaneChanged = function(pane) { if (pane == 'plugin-ingressGuard') window.plugin.ingressGuard.getPlayerAchievements; else if (pane == 'plugin-ingressGuard-Search') window.plugin.ingressGuard.searchDialog(); else $('#ingressGuard').remove() }; window.plugin.ingressGuard.versionCheck = function() { var loc_v = plugin_info.script.version; $.ajax({ url: "//ingress-guard.tk/version", type: 'GET', cache: false, crossDomain: true, dataType: 'json', }).done( function(response) { var rem_v = response.v; if (loc_v != rem_v) { dialog({ title: 'Please Update Ingress-Guard plugin', html: '

Go to Plugin site and get new version of the script

' + '

If you want use this version, just close this dialog.

', }); } } ); } var setup = function() { plugin.ingressGuard.versionCheck(); plugin.ingressGuard.iconEnl70 = L.Icon.Default.extend({ options: { iconUrl:
